<section  class='av_textblock_section av-3dpa63f-f722a48ebda062a2e111db89b6174039 '  ><div class='avia_textblock av_inherit_color' ><h1>ADELAIDE WEDDING PHOTOGRAPHERS &#038; VIDEOGRAPHERS</h1>
<p>Calm when it matters, quietly encouraging when you need it, and always there to make the day feel easy.</p>
</div></section>
<div  class='avia-button-wrap av-3adx6qj-ab65708bfd48903dfd41e5b9b0b00211-wrap avia-button-center  avia-builder-el-2  el_after_av_textblock  avia-builder-el-last '><a href='#contact'  class='avia-button av-3adx6qj-ab65708bfd48903dfd41e5b9b0b00211 av-link-btn avia-icon_select-no avia-size-medium avia-position-center avia-color-theme-color'   aria-label="CHECK IF WE’RE FREE FOR YOUR DATE!"><span class='avia_iconbox_title' >CHECK IF WE’RE FREE FOR YOUR DATE!</span></a></div>
</div></div></main></div></div></div><div id='after_section_1'  class='main_color av_default_container_wrap container_wrap fullsize'  ><div class='container av-section-cont-open' ><div class='template-page content  av-content-full alpha units'><div class='post-entry post-entry-type-page post-entry-2155'><div class='entry-content-wrapper clearfix'>
<div  class='flex_column av-38b3uuz-f9cb5b24d91703f87ac5f5185d684e26 av_three_fifth  avia-builder-el-3  el_after_av_section  el_before_av_two_fifth  avia-builder-el-first  first flex_column_div  '     ><section  id="faq-who"  class='av_textblock_section av-15n3pn-e0219f0be9fd33254e28b11ef9f144e9 '  ><div class='avia_textblock' ><h2 style="text-align: center;">Fun, Natural Wedding Photographer &amp; Videographer based in Adelaide</h2>
<p data-start="134" data-end="324">Hey there! We’re Steven and Luisa — your husband-and-wife wedding team at SvenStudios</p>
<p data-start="326" data-end="524" data-is-last-node="" data-is-only-node="">We focus on real moments — the laughter, the tears, the quiet glances, and the wonderfully chaotic bits in between. No stiff poses. No fake smiles. Just natural moments — with a bit of laughter, silliness, and good vibes thrown in.</p>
<p data-start="326" data-end="524" data-is-last-node="" data-is-only-node="">If that sounds like your style, we’d love to be part of your day!</p>
</div></section></div><div  class='flex_column av-35559yj-d931b0e69f3f6bec09bc81724384a61e av_two_fifth  avia-builder-el-5  el_after_av_three_fifth  el_before_av_one_full  flex_column_div av-parallax-object  ' data-parallax="{&quot;parallax&quot;:&quot;bottom_top&quot;,&quot;parallax_speed&quot;:&quot;4&quot;,&quot;av-desktop-parallax&quot;:&quot;inherit&quot;,&quot;av-desktop-parallax_speed&quot;:&quot;inherit&quot;,&quot;av-medium-parallax&quot;:&quot;inherit&quot;,&quot;av-medium-parallax_speed&quot;:&quot;inherit&quot;,&quot;av-small-parallax&quot;:&quot;inherit&quot;,&quot;av-small-parallax_speed&quot;:&quot;inherit&quot;,&quot;av-mini-parallax&quot;:&quot;inherit&quot;,&quot;av-mini-parallax_speed&quot;:&quot;inherit&quot;,&quot;parallax-container&quot;:&quot;.av-35559yj-d931b0e69f3f6bec09bc81724384a61e&quot;}"    ><div  class='avia-image-container av-333qqsb-7dbef0cc1cc9fdfbfe7ece10777d2a58 av-styling-circle avia-align-center  avia-builder-el-6  avia-builder-el-no-sibling '  ><div class="avia-image-container-inner"><div class="avia-image-overlay-wrap"><img decoding="async" fetchpriority="high" class="wp-image-56037 avia-img-lazy-loading-not-56037 avia_image " src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20352%20352'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="SvenStudios Photographers" title="svenstudios photographers" height="352" width="352" data-lazy-src="https://i0.wp.com/svenstudios.com/dir/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/image-description.gif?fit=352%2C352&#038;ssl=1"><noscript><img decoding="async" fetchpriority="high" class="wp-image-56037 avia-img-lazy-loading-not-56037 avia_image " src="https://i0.wp.com/svenstudios.com/dir/wp-content/uploads/2025/09/image-description.gif?fit=352%2C352&amp;ssl=1" alt="SvenStudios Photographers" title="svenstudios photographers" height="352" width="352"></noscript></div></div></div></div></p>
<div  class='flex_column av-m69w52fq-86be8bb2c0c7217eaf9558668a17ca26 av_one_full  avia-builder-el-7  el_after_av_two_fifth  el_before_av_section  avia-builder-el-last  first flex_column_div av-parallax-object  ' data-parallax="{&quot;parallax&quot;:&quot;bottom_top&quot;,&quot;parallax_speed&quot;:&quot;4&quot;,&quot;av-desktop-parallax&quot;:&quot;inherit&quot;,&quot;av-desktop-parallax_speed&quot;:&quot;inherit&quot;,&quot;av-medium-parallax&quot;:&quot;inherit&quot;,&quot;av-medium-parallax_speed&quot;:&quot;inherit&quot;,&quot;av-small-parallax&quot;:&quot;inherit&quot;,&quot;av-small-parallax_speed&quot;:&quot;inherit&quot;,&quot;av-mini-parallax&quot;:&quot;inherit&quot;,&quot;av-mini-parallax_speed&quot;:&quot;inherit&quot;,&quot;parallax-container&quot;:&quot;.av-m69w52fq-86be8bb2c0c7217eaf9558668a17ca26&quot;}"    ><section  class='av_textblock_section av-m69vzhmh-dbbf09bd4de82dd9250fcbbf49d5a659 '  ><div class='avia_textblock' ><p style="text-align: center; font-size: 30px; color: maroon;"><em>You don’t need to know how to pose.</em></p>
<p style="text-align: center; font-size: 30px; color: maroon;"><em>You don’t need to be confident in front of a camera.</em></p>

</div></div></div></div></div></div><div id='after_section_2'  class='main_color av_default_container_wrap container_wrap fullsize'  ><div class='container av-section-cont-open' ><div class='template-page content  av-content-full alpha units'><div class='post-entry post-entry-type-page post-entry-2155'><div class='entry-content-wrapper clearfix'>
<div  class='flex_column av-2ml3umz-ba0be7c866aba63e4d9b88665b4125fc av_one_full  avia-builder-el-11  el_after_av_section  el_before_av_section  avia-builder-el-no-sibling  first flex_column_div  '     ><section  id="faq-why"  class='av_textblock_section av-2leas8r-8ddcccf40d7a15f2ed0368c19bfa6524 '  ><div class='avia_textblock' ><h2 style="text-align: center;">NO MANNEQUINS HERE &#8211; JUST <span class="sketch-underline-smaller"><em><strong>AUTHENTIC</strong></em></span> PHOTO AND VIDEO</h2>
<p style="text-align: center;">Our ultimate goal is to tell the story of the people in our images.</p>
<p style="text-align: center;">We love the unconventional, We are all about documenting love stories that are uniquely yours. Forget stiff poses or traditional shots – together, we’ll create something bold, creative, and totally reflective of who you guys are and have fun doing it!</p>
<p style="text-align: center;" data-start="326" data-end="524" data-is-last-node="" data-is-only-node="">Whether your day is a big celebration, an intimate elopement, or something beautifully unconventional, we’re there to help you relax, enjoy the day, and trust us to capture the story exactly as it unfolds.</p>
<p style="text-align: center;" data-start="326" data-end="524" data-is-last-node="" data-is-only-node="">Wedding photos and video shouldn’t just show what your day looked like — they should remind you exactly how it felt.</p>
</div></section></div>

</div></div></div></div></div><div id='after_section_3'  class='main_color av_default_container_wrap container_wrap fullsize'  ><div class='container av-section-cont-open' ><div class='template-page content  av-content-full alpha units'><div class='post-entry post-entry-type-page post-entry-2155'><div class='entry-content-wrapper clearfix'>
<div  class='flex_column av-22yp93f-26a848650edf5fb954941fae1504e309 av_one_full  avia-builder-el-15  el_after_av_section  el_before_av_section  avia-builder-el-no-sibling  first flex_column_div  '     ><section  id="faq-other"  class='av_textblock_section av-21mdpmz-69b5d823c16f98bd5286513499ce2f1c '  ><div class='avia_textblock' ><h2 style="text-align: center;">ARE YOU THINKING ‘we love this but feel awkward in front of a camera’ — YOU&#8217;RE EXACTLY WHO WE WORK WITH</h2>
<p style="text-align: center;">The hundreds of couples you see on this page felt exactly the same way at the beginning. They weren’t models, they didn’t know how to pose, and they were convinced they’d feel awkward in front of a camera.</p>
<p style="text-align: center;">THIS IS NORMAL</p>
<p style="text-align: center;">Our job isn’t to make you perform or turn your wedding into an expensive photoshoot — it’s to create a space where you can relax, be yourselves, and enjoy the day as it unfolds. We’ll gently guide when it helps, step back when moments happen naturally, and make sure everything feels easy, unforced, and true to you.</p>
</div></section>

<section  class='av_textblock_section av-mhybpj7n-1d9ce9598deca5fea74cf0579f4cd107 '  ><div class='avia_textblock av_inherit_color' ><p>Thank you so much Sven Studios for capturing our special Wedding day! We absolutely LOVE our photos and are so glad we found you to be our photographer! You were a pleasure to work with, made us feel at ease with your humour during the day, and you truly have a skill for capturing the most beautiful shots in golden hour light amongst deep green forest trees  We definitely recommend you to others getting married! – Sophia</p>

<p data-start="82" data-end="369">No hidden fees, no weird upsells – just straight-up wedding packages that actually make sense. We&#8217;re also big on doing our bit for the planet, which is why we&#8217;re proud members of ‘1% for the Planet.’ So while we’re capturing your love story, we’re also helping out Mother Earth. Win-win.</p>
<p data-start="371" data-end="659" data-is-last-node="" data-is-only-node="">Our style? Super chill and all about <em data-start="408" data-end="413">you</em>. We’re big believers that if you’re not having fun, the photos won’t hit right. We bring all the good vibes (and maybe a few dad jokes) from years of working with kids – making sure everyone feels comfy, relaxed, and ready to just enjoy the day.</p>

<div  class='flex_column av-m694e3bw-26a80e54f9e8c578c7714be354700bea av_one_full  avia-builder-el-53  el_after_av_layout_row  el_before_av_section  avia-builder-el-no-sibling  first flex_column_div  '     ><section  id="faq-travel"  class='av_textblock_section av-2c2nzv-6124e9a3d508ca75049bb89a01262d70 '  ><div class='avia_textblock' ><h2 style="text-align: center;">WHY CHOOSE US FOR YOUR WEDDING PHOTOGRAPHY AND VIDEOGRAPHY?</h2>
<p style="text-align: center;">Most weekends we are out at a wedding and enjoying every minute!</p>
<p style="text-align: center;">With us, you’re not just getting any photographer and videographer; you’re gaining partners who are as invested in your wedding as you are. We will treat your day as if we were our own wedding photographer!</p>
<p style="text-align: center;">Wherever your dream wedding takes you, we’re there to capture your unique love story. Whether it’s in our home town of <a href="https://svenstudios.com/adelaide-wedding-photographer/">Adelaide</a>, or the vineyards of <a href="https://svenstudios.com/natural-barossa-valley-wedding-photography/">Barossa Valley</a> or <a href="https://svenstudios.com/natural-mclaren-vale-wedding-photography/">McLaren Vale</a>, the vibrant cities of <a href="https://svenstudios.com/darwin-wedding-photography/">Darwin</a>, <a href="https://svenstudios.com/hobart-wedding-photography/">Hobart</a>, or <a href="https://svenstudios.com/canberra-wedding-photographer/">Canberra</a>, or even <a href="https://svenstudios.com/destination-wedding-photography/">abroad</a> (we quite like heading to <a href="https://svenstudios.com/queenstown-wedding-photography/ ">Queenstown in New Zealand</a>!), our tailored photography packages are designed to suit your day perfectly.</p>
<p style="text-align: center;">Choosing us for your wedding photography and videography means partnering with passionate people who make the experience enjoyable and stress-free. Trust us to seize the beauty and joy of your special day, leaving you with images of timeless memories to treasure forever.</p>
</div></section></div>

	(function($) {

			/*	check if google analytics tracking is disabled by user setting via cookie - or user must opt in.	*/

			var analytics_code = "\n<script async src=\"https:\/\/www.googletagmanager.com\/gtag\/js?id=G-0CKGH0RV47\"><\/script>\n<script>\n  window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];\n  function gtag(){dataLayer.push(arguments);}\n  gtag('js', new Date());\n\n  gtag('config', 'G-0CKGH0RV47');\n<\/script>".replace(/\"/g, '"' );
			var html = document.getElementsByTagName('html')[0];

			$('html').on( 'avia-cookie-settings-changed', function(e)
			{
					var cookie_check = html.className.indexOf('av-cookies-needs-opt-in') >= 0 || html.className.indexOf('av-cookies-can-opt-out') >= 0;
					var allow_continue = true;
					var silent_accept_cookie = html.className.indexOf('av-cookies-user-silent-accept') >= 0;
					var script_loaded = $( 'script.google_analytics_scripts' );

					if( cookie_check && ! silent_accept_cookie )
					{
						if( ! document.cookie.match(/aviaCookieConsent/) || html.className.indexOf('av-cookies-session-refused') >= 0 )
						{
							allow_continue = false;
						}
						else
						{
							if( ! document.cookie.match(/aviaPrivacyRefuseCookiesHideBar/) )
							{
								allow_continue = false;
							}
							else if( ! document.cookie.match(/aviaPrivacyEssentialCookiesEnabled/) )
							{
								allow_continue = false;
							}
							else if( document.cookie.match(/aviaPrivacyGoogleTrackingDisabled/) )
							{
								allow_continue = false;
							}
						}
					}

					//	allow 3-rd party plugins to hook (see enfold\config-cookiebot\cookiebot.js)
					if( window['wp'] && wp.hooks )
					{
						allow_continue = wp.hooks.applyFilters( 'aviaCookieConsent_allow_continue', allow_continue );
					}

					if( ! allow_continue )
					{
//						window['ga-disable-G-0CKGH0RV47'] = true;
						if( script_loaded.length > 0 )
						{
							script_loaded.remove();
						}
					}
					else
					{
						if( script_loaded.length == 0 )
						{
							$('head').append( analytics_code );
						}
					}
			});

			$('html').trigger( 'avia-cookie-settings-changed' );

	})( jQuery );
